<div>&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for Informatica 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Informatica Upgrade Planner has been designed and created by the Informatica Global Customer Support team to provide an insight into the Informatica product upgrades.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This interactive self-service guide provides the information required to upgrade to Informatica 10.1 version from earlier versions. In this guide, you will learn:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New features, architectural changes and steps to upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Different types of upgrade and best practices to follow during the upgrade      cycle&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade process consists of the following phases:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform      the pre-upgrade tasks/checklists&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Informatica Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Repository Service Contents&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Informatica Client Tools&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform      the post-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade steps may involve additional steps based on the version you are upgrading from. To start with the upgrade, let us understand your existing implementation. This step-by-step process can be used for upgrading to Informatica version 10.1 from the earlier versions.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;It is always recommended to run the upgrade on a development environment before upgrading the production.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select your existing Informatica version...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bca700-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bca700-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3909Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services from IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to Informatica DQ 10.1. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to IDQ 10.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bcce10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bcce10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3909Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services from IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to Informatica DQ 10.1. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to IDQ 10.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0ba5d11-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Post-installation Verification and Adding Kerberos Authentication Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the Informatica domain - Run &lt;em&gt;infasetup updategatewaynode/updateworkernode&lt;/em&gt; commands to update all gateway and worker nodes in the domain with Kerberos authentication server information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client machines -&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Copy the Kerberos configuration file and set the environment variable on the machines that host the Informatica clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;For more information refer &quot;Chapter 10: After you upgrade&amp;rdquo; &amp;nbsp;in&amp;nbsp;Informatica 10.1 &amp;ndash; Upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;guide (based on the version you are upgrading from).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the pointers to consider for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0ba5d11-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba5d11-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bad240-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bad240-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4916Font1&quot;&gt;If you plan a hardware or database upgrade while upgrading Informatica products, Informatica 10.1 has the capability to support the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;during the Upgrade Directory installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest Hotfix release of Informatica 10.1 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#a0be0690-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bdb870-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0be0690-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bdb870-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and for&amp;nbsp;Informatica 9.6.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb9590-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bb9590-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb9590-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high-level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.1 - upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_UpgradingFrom951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt; guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.1 in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain and server files for Informatica 10.1. It upgrades the tables of the domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration repository to a different database, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high-level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.1 - upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_UpgradingFrom951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt; guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.1 in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain and server files for Informatica 10.1. It upgrades the tables of the domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration repository to a different database, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb4770-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0be7bc0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New Features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a&amp;nbsp;mapplet&amp;nbsp;from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use themapplet&amp;nbsp;as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backe859a130-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e859a130-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e859a130-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bd1c30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To run the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select the option to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;section. Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If you did not select to automatically recycle services after upgrade, restart the upgraded services.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view post IDQ Service upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; The service upgrade wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3225&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3225anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If dependency errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;-&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status -&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details &lt;/em&gt;section.&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If you select not to automatically recycle services after an upgrade,&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;restart the upgraded services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;SQL Data Services Drivers&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After upgrading Informatica Data Services, upgrade the Informatica JDBC or ODBC Drivers for SQL Data Services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3300&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3300Font1&quot;&gt;To upgrade the driver, run the Informatica JDBC/ODBC driver installation program and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select the option to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;section. Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If you did not select to automatically recycle services after upgrade, restart the upgraded services.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Temporary Requirements&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The installer writes temporary files to the hard disk. Verify that you have enough available disk space on the machine to support the installation. When the installation completes, the installer deletes the temporary files and releases the disk space.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The following table lists the temporary disk space requirements during installation:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Temporary space can be specified with&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;SpellE&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spelle&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;IATempDir environment variable&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;. This is the location of temporary files created during installation. &amp;nbsp;Informatica requires 1 GB disk space for temporary files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Would like to view the steps involved in the upgrade process?&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would like to view the steps involved in the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8af60-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b8af60-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b8af60-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8af60-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8af60-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Application Services pre-upgrade checklist&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure POSIX Asynchronous I/O: If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous I/O&amp;nbsp;available on any node where you want to.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Informatica Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;You can configure the INFA_DOMAINS_FILE and INFA_HOME environment variables to store the domain and installation location settings.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Locale Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;Use LANG, LC_CTYPE, or LC_ALL to set the UNIX code page. Different UNIX operating systems require different values for the same locale. The value for the locale variable is case sensitive. For Oracle database clients, set NLS_LANG to the locale you want the database client and server to use with the login.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the Keystore File Location for the Administrator Tool:&amp;nbsp;If you used a keystore file that you created to secure the connection to the Administrator tool, you must verify the keystore file location before you access the Administrator tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Clear Browser Cache:&amp;nbsp;Before you access the Administrator tool, clear the browser cache. On Windows Internet Explorer, delete the browsing history, including temporary files, cookies, and history.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete Changing the Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;If you chose to change the node configuration during the domain upgrade because you migrated the Informatica services installation to a different machine, you must perform additional tasks before you upgrade the application services.&amp;nbsp;You must perform the following additional tasks:    </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the range of dynamic port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Application Services upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high-level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.1 - upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_UpgradingFrom951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt; guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.1 in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain and server files for Informatica 10.1. It upgrades the tables of the domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration repository to a different database, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high-level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.1 - upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_UpgradingFrom951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt; guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.1 in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain and server files for Informatica 10.1. It upgrades the tables of the domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration repository to a different database, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b972b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt; Application Services and Client Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post-upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba5d11-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba5d11-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot;
