style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b61750-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b61750-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b61750-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and for&amp;nbsp;Informatica 9.6.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No, Show me Application Service pre-upgrade checklist. &lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bb9590-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bb9590-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure POSIX Asynchronous I/O: If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous I/O&amp;nbsp;available on any node where you want to.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Informatica Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;You can configure the INFA_DOMAINS_FILE and INFA_HOME environment variables to store the domain and installation location settings.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Locale Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;Use LANG, LC_CTYPE, or LC_ALL to set the UNIX code page. Different UNIX operating systems require different values for the same locale. The value for the locale variable is case sensitive. For Oracle database clients, set NLS_LANG to the locale you want the database client and server to use with the login.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the Keystore File Location for the Administrator Tool:&amp;nbsp;If you used a keystore file that you created to secure the connection to the Administrator tool, you must verify the keystore file location before you access the Administrator tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Clear Browser Cache:&amp;nbsp;Before you access the Administrator tool, clear the browser cache. On Windows Internet Explorer, delete the browsing history, including temporary files, cookies, and history.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete Changing the Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;If you chose to change the node configuration during the domain upgrade because you migrated the Informatica services installation to a different machine, you must perform additional tasks before you upgrade the application services.&amp;nbsp;You must perform the following additional tasks:    </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the range of dynamic port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba0ef0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;9.0.1 or Prior Versions&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b74fd0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b5c930-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b74fd0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b5c930-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;WordSection1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica platform consists of a server component and one or more client components. Informatica provides separate installers to upgrade the Informatica services and clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;If the product version that is currently installed cannot be upgraded to Informatica 10.1, you must first upgrade to a supported version. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;GramE&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;To determine the Informatica product version that is currently installed, click &lt;em&gt;Help &amp;gt; About Informatica Administrator&lt;/em&gt; in the Informatica Administrator Console header area.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the prerequisites:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest Hotfix release of Informatica 10.1 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b7ec10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b7ec10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b7ec10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Process&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;The upgrade process involves the following phases:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files, run the Informatica server installer and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option. The domain upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the domain has multiple nodes, you must upgrade all nodes. When you upgrade each node in the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and Server files, log in to the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and upgrade the application services. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides a list of all applications that must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the Informatica client, run the Informatica client installer and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option. If client is installed on multiple machines, upgrade the client on all the machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the pre-installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b94ba0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b94ba0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8fd81-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;during the Upgrade Directory installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post-upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade process before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain, stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Run the Pre-installation (i10Pi) System Check Tool to verify whether the machine meets the system requirements for installation or upgrade.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating system-specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain and Server Files Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain and Server Files Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b999c0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b999c0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b999c0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b6daa0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica version 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and for&amp;nbsp;Informatica 9.6.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bad240-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba8420-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bad240-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0ba8420-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.1 from 10.0 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 10.1 fresh or while upgrading to 10.1, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Make sure you save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is&amp;nbsp;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;property for the domain in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;tool. You can also use&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;infasetup updateGatewaynode&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to update the directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory in the new installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bec9e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bec9e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bec9e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;452183b0-3f1b-11e6-a5bc-bc764e10d166&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica version 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a&amp;nbsp;mapplet&amp;nbsp;from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use themapplet&amp;nbsp;as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the prerequisites for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;The upgrade process involves the following phases:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files, run the Informatica server installer and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option. The domain upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the domain has multiple nodes, you must upgrade all nodes. When you upgrade each node in the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and Server files, log in to the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and upgrade the application services. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides a list of all applications that must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the Informatica client, run the Informatica client installer and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option. If client is installed on multiple machines, upgrade the client on all the machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica version 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the prerequisites for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b6b390-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Domain Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high-level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.1 - upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFrom961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;Upgrade from 9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_UpgradingFrom951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt; guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.1 in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain and server files for Informatica 10.1. It upgrades the tables of the domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration repository to a different database, choose to change the node configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Application Services upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba3600-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bb6e80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;No, Show me Application Service pre-upgrade checklist. &lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bd9161-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bd6a50-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bd9161-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bd6a50-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bd6a50-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bd6a50-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bd6a50-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Prerequisites&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the prerequisites:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest Hotfix release of Informatica 10.1 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to check Product Availability Matrix (PAM) for 10.1?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b86140-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b86140-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b81321-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Domain Pre-upgrade Checklist&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade process before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain, stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Run the Pre-installation (i10Pi) System Check Tool to verify whether the machine meets the system requirements for installation or upgrade.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating system-specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain and Server Files Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Domain upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Post Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the IDS upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica platform consists of a server component and one or more client components. Informatica provides separate installers to upgrade the Informatica services and clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;If the product version that is currently installed cannot be upgraded to Informatica 10.1, you must first upgrade to a supported version. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bbe3b1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bbe3b1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bc0ac0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bbbca0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b7c500-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New Major Features/Enhancements with Informatica 10.1 Release&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot;
