class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0ba8420-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba8420-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the Informatica domain - Run &lt;em&gt;infasetup updategatewaynode/updateworkernode&lt;/em&gt; commands to update all gateway and worker nodes in the domain with Kerberos authentication server information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client machines -&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Copy the Kerberos configuration file and set the environment variable on the machines that host the Informatica clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;For more information refer &quot;Chapter 10: After you upgrade&amp;rdquo; &amp;nbsp;in&amp;nbsp;Informatica 10.1 &amp;ndash; Upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;guide (based on the version you are upgrading from).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b83a30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bd9161-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b83a30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bd9161-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest Hotfix release of Informatica 10.1 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the Upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt; guide&amp;nbsp;depending on version you are upgrading from:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the Reporting and Dashboards Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare Profile Warehouse, Reference Data Warehouse/Directories, Staging and Human Task Databases.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Clear the environment variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the previous installation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b999c0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b999c0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To upgrade Informatica, complete the following pre-installation tasks before starting the upgrade:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the Upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt; guide&amp;nbsp;depending on version you are upgrading from:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the Reporting and Dashboards Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare Profile Warehouse, Reference Data Warehouse/Directories, Staging and Human Task Databases.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Clear the environment variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the previous installation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b92490-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bcf520-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;IDQ Services - Post Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IDQ Upgrade from 10.0 to 10.1&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks for the following:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain:&lt;/strong&gt; Verify&amp;nbsp;that the log events directory is correct,&amp;nbsp;Verify the SMTP configuration properties that the domain uses to send domain alerts and service alerts.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PowerCenter Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;If you upgraded from a version that used operating system profiles, set the umask setting to change the security on files that the DTM writes and if you install identity population data files, verify that the Informatica services that run mappings and sessions can find the files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Content Management Service:&lt;/strong&gt; Restart the Data Integration Service and&amp;nbsp;Analyst Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Data Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt; Activate the Workflow Orchestration Service module and configure the workflow database and recycle the services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To send email notifications for business glossaries, scorecards, and workflows, configure and enable the Email Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Analyst Service:&lt;/strong&gt; Upgrade the Business Glossary data in the Model repository and&amp;nbsp;Recycle the Analyst Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Informatica ODBC or JDBC driver on each machine from which you connect to the SQL data service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IDQ Upgrade from 9.6.1 to 10.1&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks for the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain:&lt;/strong&gt; Verify&amp;nbsp;that the log events directory is correct,&amp;nbsp;Verify the SMTP configuration properties that the domain uses to send domain alerts and service alerts and if you used your SSL certificate files to enable secure communication in the previous domain, verify the keystore and truststore file locations. The upgrade process does not update these locations.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you enabled secure communication between client applications and the previous domain, verify the keystore file locations. The upgrade process does not update these locations.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PowerCenter Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;If you upgraded from a version that used operating system profiles, set the umask setting to change the security on files that the DTM writes and&amp;nbsp;If you install identity population data files, verify that the Informatica services that run mappings and sessions can find the files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Content Management Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;If you update any property for address reference data, identity population data, classifier model data, or probabilistic model data, restart the Data Integration Service and&amp;nbsp;If you update the location of the reference data warehouse, restart the Analyst Service and the Data Integration Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Data Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;If you plan to run workflows, activate the Workflow Orchestration Service module and configure the workflow database. Before you run a workflow, recycle the service, If the Data Integration Service runs on multiple nodes and you configured the execution options differently for each service process, verify that the Execution Options on the Properties view use the correct values and&amp;nbsp;Verify that the Maximum Memory Per Request property uses the correct value for each Data Integration Service module.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Analyst Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Run the upgradeRepository command line program to upgrade the Business Glossary data in the Model repository and&amp;nbsp;Recycle the Analyst Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-index the Model Repository Service search index.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Reference Data:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;After you upgrade, complete the post-upgrade tasks for reference data objects and files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Profiles:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Migrate Profile and Scorecard Results and Import Data Domains&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IDQ Upgrade from 9.5.1 to 10.1&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks for the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;The Informatica installation includes DataDirect 7.1 ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers if you upgrade from Informatica 9.5.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PowerCenter Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt; Configure Umask for Operating System Profiles and Verify the Location of the Identity Population Files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Content Management Service:&lt;/strong&gt; Verify the Location Identity Population files, Restart service&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Data Integration Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Reset the HTTP Proxy Server Password,&amp;nbsp;Verify the Workflow&amp;nbsp;Orchestration Service module is active and identify the workflow database.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Analyst Service:&lt;/strong&gt; The Data Director Service is converted to an Analyst Service. You may view two Analyst Services when the upgrade is complete.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Update the Metadata Manager properties file to include any customization,&amp;nbsp;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool,&amp;nbsp;Verify Load privileges and permissions for Metadata Manager users and&amp;nbsp;If a secure connection is configured for the Metadata Manager web application, verify the truststore file for the mmcmd and mmRepoCmd command line programs.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Human Task Properties&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you upgrade a domain that includes a Data Director Service, the upgrade operation converts the Data Director Service to an Analyst Service. The Analyst Service uses the Data Integration Service properties from the Data Director Service to update the Human task properties. Any user who worked on Human task instances in Informatica Data Director for Data Quality can log into the Analyst Service URL to work on the task instances.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you upgrade services in a domain that contains an Analyst Service and a Data Director Service, the domain contains two Analyst Services when the upgrade operation is complete. You can maintain the two services, or you can merge the properties to a single Analyst Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Reference Data:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;After you upgrade, complete the post-upgrade tasks for reference data objects and files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Profiles and Scorecards:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Migrate Profile data domain discovery, Scorecard Results, and Import Data Domains.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the names of the workflows and associated objects in the Model repository.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bcf520-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bcf520-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bcf520-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bddf80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and for&amp;nbsp;Informatica 9.6.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#a0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b88850-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b8fd80-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b88850-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;WordSection1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Minimum Requirements&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The following table describes the minimum system requirements for a domain with different node configurations:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table class=&quot;MsoTableGrid&quot; border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; width=&quot;719&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;315&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Services&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;143&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Processor&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;126&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Memory&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;136&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Disk Space&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;315&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;One node runs the following services:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst&quot;&gt;&lt;!--[if !supportLists]--&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp;-&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Analyst Service&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Temporary Requirements&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The installer writes temporary files to the hard disk. Verify that you have enough available disk space on the machine to support the installation. When the installation completes, the installer deletes the temporary files and releases the disk space.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The following table lists the temporary disk space requirements during installation:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Temporary space can be specified with&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;SpellE&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spelle&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;IATempDir environment variable&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;. This is the location of temporary files created during installation. &amp;nbsp;Informatica requires 1 GB disk space for temporary files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#a0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ba5d10-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b9c0d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to IDQ 10.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0b94ba0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Pre-installation Tasks&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To upgrade Informatica, complete the following pre-installation tasks before starting the upgrade:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the Upgrading from &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.5.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion951_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.5.1&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom9.6.1&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion961_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a title=&quot;UpgradingFrom10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_UpgradingFromVersion100_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt; guide&amp;nbsp;depending on version you are upgrading from:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the Reporting and Dashboards Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare Profile Warehouse, Reference Data Warehouse/Directories, Staging and Human Task Databases.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Clear the environment variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the previous installation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Domain upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b94ba0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b999c1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0b94ba0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Path for upgrade from v9.1.0 to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade from 9.1.0 to 10.1 is not supported. You must first upgrade 9.1.0 to supported version 9.6.1 and then you would be able to upgrade to 10.1.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For information on upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1, refer the &lt;a href=&quot;../conversation/?id=44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for 9.6.1&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Do you want to take a look at the new features in Informatica 10.1?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0b701b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b701b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0b701b0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bd9160-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New Major Features/Enhancements with Informatica 10.0 Release&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 10.0 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;10.0&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the prerequisites for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to IDQ 10.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bc58e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc58e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc58e0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;IDS Upgrade Process&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3197Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services IDS 9.5.1, 9.6.1 or 10.0 to Informatica DS 10.1. The service upgrade wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3225&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3225anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If dependency errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;-&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status -&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details &lt;/em&gt;section.&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If you select not to automatically recycle services after an upgrade,&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;restart the upgraded services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;SQL Data Services Drivers&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After upgrading Informatica Data Services, upgrade the Informatica JDBC or ODBC Drivers for SQL Data Services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3300&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3300Font1&quot;&gt;To upgrade the driver, run the Informatica JDBC/ODBC driver installation program and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the IDQ Services upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bc7ff0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bc7ff0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0bc31d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0b83a30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0b83a30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the prerequisites:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest Hotfix release of Informatica 10.1 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#a0b5a220-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0be2da0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a0baab30-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Pointers to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.1 from 10.0 or Prior Version&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.1 from 10.0 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 10.1 fresh or while upgrading to 10.1, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Make sure you save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is&amp;nbsp;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;property for the domain in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;tool. You can also use&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;infasetup updateGatewaynode&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to update the directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory in the new installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Advance Upgrade options in Informatica 10.1?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a0bea2d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a0be54b1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0bea2d0-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#a0be54b1-3ca4-11e6-87fc-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica introduces Intelligent Data Lake, a new product to help customers derive more value from their Hadoop-based data lake and make data available to all users in the organization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Scheduler Service to schedule profile runs and scorecard runs to run at a specific time or intervals&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Effective in version 10.1, you can use Sqoop to process data between relational databases and HDFS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import mappings that contain Netezza and Teradata objects from PowerCenter into the Developer tool and run the mappings in a native or Hadoop run-time environment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From version 10.1, you can generate a mapplet from a group of connected transformations in a mapping. Use the mapplet as a template to add to multiple mappings that connect to different sources and targets.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sqoop Connectivity for Relational Sources and Targets&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Push mappings to the Apache Spark engine in the Hadoop environment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary like Inherit Glossary Content Managers to All Assets,&amp;nbsp;Bi-directional Custom Relationships and&amp;nbsp;Custom Colors in the Relationship View Diagram&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Monitor tab in the Administrator tool&amp;nbsp;has been enhanced with execution Statics view, historical Statistics view.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;An application can call the Data Transformation REST API to run a Data Transformation service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Version 10.1 onwards, you can customize the cipher suites that the Informatica domain uses for secure communication within the domain and secure connections to web application services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation contains additional address functionality for several countries including Germany, South Korea, UK, France, Ireland and many more countries.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters like Kerberos authentication for native Greenplum&amp;nbsp;connections.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10.1 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/5/IN_101_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
